Confrontation Between Chinese and Japanese Military Police in Wanbaoshan 87

Japanese Military Police Concentrate 700 Personnel

Japanese Police on the South Manchurian Railway Line Await Mobilization Orders

Japanese Consul's Reply Contains Strong Words and Unreasonable Arguments

Changchun dispatch: After the Wanbaoshan incident occurred, on the 2nd and 3rd, Japanese military police successively went to support, totaling 500 personnel. Together with the military police who arrived in Wanbaoshan earlier, there were more than 700 personnel in total. They are now stationed in the rice paddy area and inside and outside the town. Zhou Yuping, the Director of the Municipal Government and concurrently the Director of the Foreign Affairs Office, and Ma Zhongyuan, the County Magistrate, believing that Japan was destroying Sino-Japanese relations, specially dispatched Tang Yuheng, the Chief of the Security Corps, and Lu Qi, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, to lead 350-360 police and security personnel to protect the victimized Chinese people and stop the illegal actions of the Japanese military police. Lu departed with his team around 10:00 AM on the 2nd, and Tang led his team to support at 8:00 AM on the 3rd. However, around 9:00 AM on the morning of the 4th, the Japanese side again sent 40-50 soldiers. Our side also sent Hu Qingfeng, the captain of the mounted patrol team, to lead 30 mounted patrolmen, and Fu Kui, the captain of the security team, to lead 50 cavalrymen, all under the command of the County Magistrate, to go directly to Wanbaoshan to reinforce. According to a telephone report at 4:38 PM on the 4th, our military police had all arrived. The Japanese army's plan to go to the villages to collect firearms from the farmers filling the ditches was dispelled because our police and security personnel were concentrated for monitoring and refused based on reason. However, the Chinese and Japanese military police are stationed in the rice paddy area and Wanbaoshan town, forming a confrontational situation. Director Lu and Chief Tang demanded that the Nakamura team of the Japanese army return to Changchun together with their team to await instructions from their superiors. They replied that they would not withdraw until the case was concluded and they received orders, and that if the Chinese people gathered again to fill the ditches, they would be dealt with by force.

On the afternoon of the 3rd, Japanese residents in Changchun held a Wanbaoshan Korean Farmers Support Association meeting at the Yoshino-cho Performing Arts Hall, organized by the Japanese Youth Association of Toutaogou and the Changchun branch of the Kenjidan. In addition to the leaders of various institutions, there were also all members of the Changchun branch of the Japanese Autonomous Alliance in Manchuria, students from commercial schools, and thirty or more Japanese women, totaling 140 Japanese and Koreans. Many resolutions were passed at the meeting, and the content was quite secret. On the same day, the Police Bureau of the Kwantung Government also telegraphed the Japanese police stations along the Princess Ling, Kaiyuan, Sipingjie, and Tieling lines, ordering them to each select ten elite personnel within the shortest period of time to reinforce Changchun and participate in the operation in Wanbaoshan. Upon receiving the telegram, the above police stations immediately complied. In addition, the Japanese garrison stationed in Toutaogou also received a telegram from the Japanese consul ordering them to prepare for deployment and go to Wanbaoshan in the shortest period of time to provide support for the Japanese police.

When the Wanbaoshan incident occurred, Toshiro, the Japanese consul in Changchun, immediately received two letters from Zhou Yuping, the Director of the Municipal Government on our side, proposing negotiations. Toshiro initially ignored the letters and finally replied with one letter, filled with strong words and unreasonable arguments, which is excerpted below to show the Japanese people's cunning: "To the esteemed Zhou, Director of the Changchun Municipal Government Preparatory Office: Regarding the Sanxingpu Farm issue, yesterday, July 1st, a staff member was dispatched based on a report from that area to convey the events of the violent actions of your country's farmers. Although we previously notified your side, there was no intention to suppress the rioters, and we had no choice but to dispatch appropriate police to protect the Korean farmers. However, according to subsequent reports, a hundred farmers from your country suddenly destroyed the embankment construction and filled the ditches. The police previously dispatched by our side stopped the Korean farmers' resistance in order to avoid conflicts between the two sides. It was found that when the rioters went to the scene at 10:00 AM on July 1st, Tian Xizhan, the Chief of the Second Public Security Sub-bureau of your country, was present with seven policemen to stop the farmers' riot, but they were beaten by them. Based on this kind of violent behavior, our police cannot but take self-defense measures when it is unavoidable. We hope that your side will take complete measures to vigorously stop the farmers' violent behavior. In addition, according to the Korean farmers' request, the damages suffered by the farmers due to the destruction of the embankments and filling of the ditches will be investigated later. We kindly request negotiations, etc. Addressed to Zhou, Director of the Changchun Municipal Government Preparatory Office, July 2nd, Showa 6th year, [signed] Toshiro, Consul stationed in Changchun." At the same time, the Japanese consul also requested the Municipal Government to allow the establishment of a temporary telephone line between Wanbaoshan and Changchun to facilitate communication. After hearing the situation, Director Zhou of the Municipal Government replied with the most humorous words, saying, "Our Ministry of Foreign Affairs plans to extend the Beining Railway directly to Tokyo, Japan. I wonder if the Japanese diplomatic authorities can approve it." The Japanese consul was ashamed and speechless. This is truly due to the lack of Japanese diplomatic talent and their unfamiliarity with international law, and it also shows their contempt for our country's sovereignty. (July 4th)

Xinjiang Refuses Yellow Race Inspection Group 88

No Legal Person Allowed to Enter

The Group Currently Lingering Near Yumen

Tianjin News: Guang Lu, the representative of the Xinjiang Provincial Government stationed in Beijing, recently came to Tianjin on official business. Yesterday, he received a telegram from Jin Shuren, the new Chairman of Xinjiang, stating that the Yellow Race Inspection Group would be strictly refused entry. The previous rumor that the group had already entered Xinjiang was fabricated. The original telegram is as follows: "Guang Ji Gaojian, the Yan telegram is received. Ma Zhongying's bandit remnants, totaling two to three hundred people, have lost all their arms and supplies. We have mobilized to strictly prevent them. Even if they want to flee west, they are not to be feared. Xinjiang's welcoming or refusing the Academic Investigation Group of 19 depends entirely on the government's orders and public opinion. There is no single welcome to the French side. Bu An's counter-espionage is a fabrication. The original telegram will not be difficult to expose. Chu was deceived, which is truly negligent. We have already telegraphed to investigate and stop it. No legal person is allowed to enter. Please disclose this telegram to avoid misunderstandings. Chairman Jin Shuren Dong Wu Print."

Beiping News: The Ancient Relics Preservation Committee yesterday received a telegram from Jin Shuren, Chairman of the Xinjiang Provincial Government, reporting that the Sino-French Inspection Group is still lingering near Yumen, repeatedly requesting entry into Xinjiang, but has been refused. The original telegram is as follows: "To Qian Mengcai, Brother of the Beiping Ancient Relics Preservation Committee: The Sino-French Inspection Group is still lingering near Yumen, repeatedly telegraphed, requesting entry. We have strictly refused it. As for the French side's publicity that Xinjiang welcomes legal persons, that is not the case. It is clearly a provocation. Ma Zhongying's troops have been severely attacked, and now there are only three to four hundred people left, unable to do anything. Special announcement, Jin Shuren Dong, (July 8th)"

Foreign Minister Wang Receives Press 89

Telegrams Ambassador Wang stationed in Japan to inspect Korea

Wan Incident assigned special commissioners to solve together

Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting received reporters from all newspaper agencies at 11 a.m. on the tenth, briefing the press on recent diplomatic activities. (1) Agreement to take back the Shanghai French Concession, signature would take place within the following week. Restructuring would be done after signing. The current Ministry of Justice and Administration has been preparing restructuring procedures. (2) Agreement on commerce treaty between China and Turkey, both parties have decided on a draft that the Turkish acting minister has sent by air to Turkey. Signature would take place after receiving telegram. (3) China Poland treaty has gone into effect from yesterday. The government has decided to establish an embassy in Poland, and to establish an embassy in Czech, and have the stationed-Poland ambassador concurrently manage that of Czech. Selection of personnel is ongoing. (4) Delegates of the International League have already been decided to be Minister Shi, Minister Jiang, and Vice-Minister Wang of this office. Current Minister Shi is in London, and Minister Jiang and Vice-Minister Wang are planning on leaving the country at the start of next month. Vice-Minister Wang is, in addition to attending the International League, also going to inspect various Chinese embassies and consulates overseas. (5) After the events in Korea, the Japanese government has declared its extreme regret and promise to stop immediately. To our country's protests, Lin came out to verbally reply in Beijing, and expressed an apology. Reports currently state that the stationed consulate in Korea has reported that the riots have already stopped. The foreign ministry has telegraphed to the stationed ambassador Wang in Japan to go to Korea to inspect damage reports and console the affected compatriots. After the matter is completed, he will come to Beijing to report everything. The government deeply laments the damages incurred by our compatriots this time, and are in addition to ongoing talks, thinking up ways to care for the compatriots. (6) For the Wanbaoshan Incident, the foreign ministry has instructed the Jilin special commissioner to, together with the Jilin Provincial Government, to find solutions. The central government will put in its utmost effort to help the locality to solve this matter. (7) The Consul General stationed in Korea, Lu Chunfang, has other duties and has yet to complete them, and is expected to be stationed after the completion. (8) Selection of personnel for the ambassador stationed in America is ongoing. (9) China-America Rights and Benefits cases are already en route. After receipt, the American ambassador will come to Beijing. (10) The speaker will travel to Qingdao Weihai within the day, after which the meeting will adjourn.

Jiang Annihilation of Red Army Approaching Bandit Nests 90

Majority of Red Bandits Still Defending Old Nest

Nanchang dispatch: News was received from the front lines that other than the fact that one contingent of red bandits are attempting to escape to Min territory, the majority are still defending the old nests. Zhu Mao's main force has gathered in Guangchang Ningdu Xingguo Shicheng Ruijin Huichang regions, and its important units, such as the fake Soviet and fake military commission, are situated in Ningdu Guangchang county town, as well as the bandit dens like Luokou Xiaobu Longgang Donggu Chenggang Shaxi Futian Baisha etc. The bandit front lines are located at the border of Lean and Ningdu in Zhaoxie, border of Nanfeng and Guangchang in Qia Village, as well as Hengshi in Yihuang, Yaotian in Yongfeng, Shuikou and Baisha in Jishui, Futian in Jian, Guobei in Taihe. After the annihilation of the red armies in Nanfeng, the red bandits were at a loss, and fled to Southern Jiang and Western Min, hence the extremely quick progress made by the left wing, with the annihilation of the bandit army of Lichuan already breaking out of the Min border, and the various armies in Nanfeng pressing on Guangchang, and Kangdu could be retaken. After retaking this area, the various red bandit gangs of Jianning in Fujian, and Ningdu Guangchang Nanfeng in Jiangxi, could no longer link up. The central route is trying to take Ningdu, the right wing attacking Futian Shuikou and Yaotian, having already reached the bandit region and pressing closer to the bandits' positions.

News Continued

Jinan Again Searches for Qian Wencan's Remains 91

Another Page of the Tragic History of the May 3rd Massacre

Jinan Correspondence: The May 3rd Massacre saw countless Chinese citizens killed. Moreover, the Japanese army always moved and destroyed corpses after committing atrocities. Therefore, to this day, the exact number of martyrs remains unknown. Cai Gongshi, a diplomat, was martyred at the old Diplomatic Affairs Office. Recently, Mrs. Cai came to Shandong to search for his remains. Excavation resulted in only a pile of charred bones and several lumps of burnt flesh. Now, the family of Qian Wencan is also requesting exhumation. The process is recorded as follows:

A week before the May 3rd Massacre, an event ignited the tragedy. On April 26th, two Japanese soldiers were swaggering eastward on Jing Si Road, west of Jinan Commercial Port Park. Suddenly, a person in plainclothes fired a pistol at them from behind in an assassination attempt. The assassin then fled into the park. It was rumored at the time that the attacker was actually a Chinese rogue hired by the Japanese to provide a pretext. Consequently, the Japanese implemented a full-scale emergency curfew in the city starting on April 26th, inspecting pedestrians with extreme violence. At this time, Qian Wencan, a linesman from the Jinan Telegraph Bureau, finished his work in the western part of the commercial port and was returning to the bureau by car. Unexpectedly, he was stopped by the Japanese army for inspection. Because Qian did not understand Japanese, he was arrested and taken to Donglu Middle School, south of Sanlizhuang, as the school was occupied by the Japanese army at the time and used as a garrison headquarters. From then on, Qian disappeared. The Telegraph Bureau tried every means to rescue him, but the Japanese army flatly denied knowing anything. It was not until the Japanese army withdrew in the 18th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1929] that the Telegraph Bureau and Qian's family went to Donglu Middle School to search. However, when the school was occupied, all the staff had been driven away, and the files had been burned, making it impossible to investigate. The mysterious case remained unresolved. To commemorate this case, the Telegraph Bureau erected a monument at Jinpu Station with the inscription "Although the barbarians' bombs are fierce, the spirit of the martyrs is immortal," to commemorate the martyr Qian. In September of the 18th year [1929], when Donglu Middle School reopened, it was full of rubble and severely damaged. Workers were hired to repair the damage. At that time, Qian's family and friends went to the school to search, but found nothing. This year, Mrs. Cai Gongshi came to Jinan to excavate the remains of the martyrs, and obtained many bones. Qian Wencan's wife, Qian Yu Peiyuan (from Jiangsu), was touched by this and also wanted to come to Shandong to search. She entrusted Yu Bangnai, the business manager of the Jinan Telegraph Bureau, and Lu Yaoxi of the Yanji Telegraph Main Line Works Office of the Ministry of Communications, to contact Donglu School. Principal Zhu Jinggu of the school, considering this a matter of national humiliation, readily agreed. Mr. Lu and Mr. Yu then requested the Jinan Telegraph Bureau Works Office to issue an official letter. Donglu has replied, requesting that the excavation be carried out during the summer vacation to avoid interfering with school affairs. (July 9th)

Dangerous Situations Occur in the Upper and Lower Reaches of the Yellow River in Shandong 92

Jinan Correspondence: In recent days, the water level in the upper reaches of the Yellow River has risen sharply. Fortunately, the spring embankments are still intact, preventing a breach. However, the south bank of Liuzhuang was hit by a strong current, which was extremely turbulent. The Kaibao [brushwood and earth dams] were washed away, and the dam collapsed, creating a very dangerous situation. Zhang Lianjia, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, is inspecting the upper reaches. The Cao Prefecture Eight County River Works Promotion Association sent an urgent telegram to the province yesterday (the 7th), requesting funds and materials for emergency repairs. The relevant letters and telegrams are recorded below: (1) The River Works Committee's letter stated: "To the Director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau and Standing Committee Member of the River Works Committee, Zhang: We have received an urgent telegram from the Cao Prefecture Eight County River Works Promotion Association stating that the south bank of the Yellow River in Liuzhuang is being hit by a strong current, the water level has risen by four feet, two sections of Kaibao have been washed away, and the dam has collapsed. They urgently request funds for emergency repairs, etc. In addition to promptly convening a meeting to discuss solutions, we are sending a copy of the telegram for your review. Respectfully yours, Shandong River Affairs Bureau." (2) The River Works Promotion Association's telegram stated: "To Chairman Han of the Provincial Government, Director Li of the Department of Civil Affairs, Director Zhang of the Department of Construction, Director Wang of the Department of Finance, Director He of the Department of Education, Director Wang of the Department of Agriculture and Mining, and All Members of the Provincial River Works Committee: The south bank of the Yellow River in Liuzhuang is being hit by a strong current, the water level has risen by four feet, two sections of Kaibao have been washed away, and the dam has collapsed. There are no materials or funds, and the situation is critical. We urgently request that funds be allocated for emergency repairs to protect the lives of the people. We are extremely anxious. The Cao Prefecture Eight County River Works Promotion Association kowtows."

Dangerous situations have also occurred in the lower reaches. Urgent telegrams have been received from the downstream sections, stating: (1) "To Director Zhang of the River Affairs Bureau: According to the report from the Third Flood Season Defense, due to heavy rain in recent days, there are a total of twenty-six wave nests caused by the erosion of the newly added Hou Chuang and the dam foundation at Wu Yangjia. Each wave nest requires about five or six fen of soil. As the project lacks foundation protection, erosion and wave nests are unavoidable. In addition to ordering the section to quickly fill and reinforce to prevent accidents, we respectfully report this. Li Fuchang, Section Chief of the Fifth Section of the Lower North, kowtows." (2) "To Director Zhang of the River Affairs Bureau: We have inspected the Guiren East New Shoal in this section. Since spring, it has eroded, collapsing a width of five zhang and a length of over one hundred zhang. The remaining root filling is only two zhang. The current has become slightly smoother. A total of five hundred and thirty-six old willow saplings that had survived on the shoal have been washed away. We respectfully report this for your review. Li Fuchang, Section Chief of the Fifth Section of the Lower North, kowtows." (3) "To Director Zhang of the River Affairs Bureau: We have inspected the sixteenth tier of rock protection downstream of the Buddha Head Temple dike. It has now been completely washed away, damaging the dike body. We plan to build four new sections of attached brushwood dike to resist the current and prevent major risks. We respectfully report this. Zhou Yumei, Section Chief of the Fourth Section of the Lower South, kowtows." (July 8th)

Continued Reports on the Tragic Flood Situation in Northern Guangdong 93

The Counties of Yingde and Qingyuan Have Become Vast Expanse of Water

Many Drownings and Collapsed Houses; Flood Victims Deprived of Food

Guangzhou Correspondence: Previous reports have briefly described the floods in the northwest rivers of Guangdong Province. Further investigation reveals that the disaster in the North River is particularly severe. According to a telegram from the Yingde section chief of the Yuehan Railway, the area around the Yingde branch line has been flooded. Moreover, at piling position number 3497, Lan Mountain has collapsed, preventing train passage. The subgrade on the upper section of the Pajiang has collapsed for over 400 feet. At piling position number 610 in Pajiang, the subgrade has collapsed for over 1,000 feet. At Bancun, the subgrade has collapsed for over 2,000 feet. The electricity poles in that area have been washed away by the water. The villages of Pajiang have become a watery world. The water level in Caotang Market is rising further. Bridges and markets near Yuantan have been flooded. The water level is still rising at a rate of three inches per hour. According to refugees, this flood in the northwest rivers is the worst in ten years, as tragic as the disaster in the year of Yimao [1915]. Along the North River, from Yingde downstream to Bolokeng, Lidong, Hengshi, and Pajiang, the area has become a vast expanse of water, reaching depths of seventeen or eighteen feet in some places and eight or nine feet in shallower areas. Village houses have been flooded up to the roofs, and countless houses have collapsed. Refugees are camping on the mountains, their cries shaking the wilderness, and deaths are occurring one after another. In Yuantan, over a hundred refugees have no place to live and have gathered in a nearby broken brick kiln. The kiln walls suddenly collapsed, burying over a hundred refugees alive, with no survivors. On the 30th, over twenty houses collapsed in Yuantan, drowning dozens of men and women, whose bodies floated away with the current. In Qingyuan County, the floodwaters suddenly rose by over twelve feet starting on the 29th. The upper and lower Guo Streets in Qingyuan City have become a watery world. The area in front of the county government is over a foot deep. The affiliated Zhoushin, Jiangkou, Feishikou, and Shantang areas have water levels matching the eaves of the houses. Livestock and paddy fields have been completely submerged. Rafts of fir wood (used for timber) moored on the river have been washed away, causing tens of thousands of dollars in losses to various timber shops. In Shantang Township, over twenty houses were knocked down by fir wood rafts. Rice and grain within the city have run out. A special envoy came to the province one day to request disaster relief. The boat journey from Qingyuan to Shantang takes thirty minutes. No paddy fields can be seen along the way; only a vast expanse of water. Only the trees and grass on the hills can occasionally be seen. The landslides on the mountainside that collapsed at Bolokeng on the Yuehan Railway several days ago have now piled mud on the road, covering an area of approximately sixteen to seventeen hundred feet. Moreover, over ten thousand old railroad ties along the railway have been washed away by the water. The roadbed has been eroded by the water, forming cavities. Repair work will take at least twenty days. Through trains on the Yue Shao Railway are suspended indefinitely. In total, the losses from the North River flood to the Yue Shao Railway Bureau alone are estimated at several hundred thousand dollars. Various charitable organizations here believe that the disaster in the North River is serious and have been organizing and dispatching relief teams in recent days. The Nanyang Company relief team purchased 50,000 loaves of bread, 50 bags of rice, and a large quantity of biscuits, bait, and medicine. A team of sixty members departed along the Yuehan Railway on the morning of the 3rd. Also departing on the same day was the Fuguo Mining Company relief team, heading to Yuantan to distribute relief. It is impossible to travel beyond Yuantan because the North River is turbulent, and boats cannot sail upstream. The situation beyond Yuantan is unknown. Since yesterday, charitable institutions such as Guangzhou Convenience Hospital have formed corpse retrieval teams and have ordered a large quantity of coffins, which they are carrying to the disaster areas to recover the bodies of drowned refugees. The water level in the West River is simultaneously higher than in the North River. Disaster conditions are currently being investigated, and a detailed account will be provided in the next dispatch. (July 4th)

Shanxi Currency Continues to Plunge Wildly 94

First Discounted Lottery Redemption

Taiyuan Correspondence: Since the provincial government announced the 25% discounted consolidation method for Shanxi currency, the exchange rate between paper money and silver dollars on the market has never fallen below three yuan, and the daily market has been relatively stable. Yesterday was the first day of the new method implementation where discounted lottery redemption was conducted, but the currency price not only failed to rise due to the lottery, but also fell by 32 jiao or more per yuan in a day or two. As a result, social discussions were rampant, presenting a kind of incredible phenomenon. The newly established lottery method still sorts all the paper money issued by the provincial bank by the last two digits of their serial numbers into one hundred lots. Excluding the previously drawn lots 86, 19, and 95 which were redeemed at full value, it is now planned to divide the remaining ninety-seven lots into seven drawings, with the first drawing being thirteen lots, and subsequent drawings being fourteen lots each, to be held every five months, and is estimated to be completed in three years. All drawn lots can be redeemed from the provincial bank at 40% of their face value. Yesterday was the first day of the lottery. Around 10 o'clock, many people had gathered at the entrance of the Chamber of Commerce, blocking the road. Representatives from various institutions and the public numbered about a thousand. Around 12 o'clock, Gao Buqing, the general manager of the provincial bank, announced the opening of the meeting. Xing Fenggang, the representative of the provincial government, was elected chairman, and briefly explained the lottery procedures. Thirteen people were randomly selected from the audience to draw one lot each. The numbers drawn were 98, 96, 82, 75, 66, 62, 57, 49, 39, 30, 25, 34, 79, etc. However, the drawn lots only differed from the current price by 40 jiao per yuan, and in practice, they only differed from the undrawn notes by a few fen of silver dollars per yuan, so it was not particularly noticed by the general public. The most concerning issue for society is still whether the currency price can be stabilized. Yesterday, the reporter visited a gentleman from the financial sector and asked about the reason for the continuous decline in the price of provincial currency in recent days. According to the conversation, although the financial consolidation method decided by the provincial government is not perfect, in Shanxi, which is currently facing financial difficulties, it can be considered a relatively good method. If all parties can prioritize the overall welfare and remove the previous bad ideas of only knowing private interests and disregarding the overall situation, then the financial situation of the entire province can gradually stabilize. However, all parties are not doing this, and are instead intensifying their pursuit of individualistic gains. Although there are many reasons for the decline of the provincial currency in the past, manipulation by a small number of powerful figures in the financial sector is the main reason. For example, on a certain day, the provincial bank sold 200,000 silver dollars, but ordinary businesses did not dare to intervene, and only certain businesses connected to the banking authorities purchased as much as possible, causing the currency price to fall sharply. If the provincial authorities only know how to verbally prohibit this, the result will only be that ordinary people suffer, while large businesses with sufficient financial resources and access to information will take advantage of the situation and earn even greater profits, etc. (July 6th)

Hunan Disaster Relief Lottery Issues Two Types 95

Type A First Prize is 30,000 Yuan

Type B First Prize is 20,000 Yuan

Changsha Correspondence: In order to relieve the Hunan disaster, He Jian, in consultation with various gentry and merchants, decided to organize the Hunan Disaster Relief Association and issue 3 million yuan of Hunan Disaster Relief Lottery tickets, to be issued over six months, with 500,000 yuan issued each month. Fan Chunfu was appointed as the director and Shu Jiangzhen as the deputy director. A bureau was established in Hankou to promote sales to major ports along the Yangtze River. These lottery tickets were underwritten by the Hankou Dade Company at 80% of their face value, with 30% allocated as prize money, and the government receiving 50%, equivalent to 1.5 million yuan, with the government receiving 250,000 yuan per month. The unwinning tickets will be exchanged for Hunan Disaster Relief interest-free public bonds, which will be redeemed by lottery after five years and paid off in ten years. All issuance regulations were approved by the provincial affairs meeting on July 3rd and are divided into Type A and Type B. The prize drawing date for the first period of Type A tickets is set for August 15th, and the prize drawing date for Type B tickets is set for August 30th. Afterwards, prize drawings will be held on the 15th and 30th or 31st of each month until six periods have been completed.

Type A Lottery Tickets 96

30,000 tickets are issued each month, and each ticket is divided into ten shares, with each share selling for one silver dollar, totaling 300,000 silver dollars. The prize levels and amounts are as follows: First prize, one ticket, receives a prize of 30,000 yuan; Second prize, one ticket, receives 5,000 yuan; Third prize, one ticket, receives 3,000 yuan; Fourth prize, one ticket, receives 1,000 yuan; Fifth prize, one ticket, receives 500 yuan; Sixth prize, five tickets, receive 100 yuan each, totaling 500 yuan; Seventh prize, fifty tickets, receive 30 yuan each, totaling 1,500 yuan; Eighth prize, two hundred tickets, receive 15 yuan each, totaling 3,000 yuan; Ninth prize, one thousand two hundred tickets, receive 12 yuan each, totaling 14,400 yuan; Tenth prize, three thousand tickets, receive 10 yuan each, totaling 30,000 yuan. Side prizes total 90,000 yuan. In total, Type A lottery tickets total 30,000, generating an income of 300,000 yuan. After deducting 30% for prize money (90,000 yuan) and the underwriting company's 20% discount (60,000 yuan), totaling 150,000 yuan, the government receives 150,000 yuan.

Type B Lottery Tickets 97

40,000 tickets are issued each month, and each ticket is divided into ten shares, with each share selling for half a silver dollar, totaling 200,000 silver dollars. The prize levels and amounts are as follows: First prize, one ticket, receives a prize of 20,000 yuan; Second prize, one ticket, receives 3,000 yuan; Third prize, one ticket, receives 1,500 yuan; Fourth prize, one ticket, receives 800 yuan; Fifth prize, one ticket, receives 400 yuan; Sixth prize, five tickets, receive 50 yuan each, totaling 250 yuan; Seventh prize, fifty tickets, receive 20 yuan each, totaling 1,000 yuan; Eighth prize, three hundred tickets, receive 8 yuan each, totaling 2,400 yuan; Ninth prize, one thousand six hundred tickets, receive 6 yuan each, totaling 9,600 yuan; Tenth prize, four thousand tickets, receive 5 yuan each, totaling 20,000 yuan. Side prizes total 60,000 yuan. In total, Type B lottery tickets total 40,000, generating an income of 200,000 yuan. After deducting 30% for prize money (60,000 yuan) and the underwriting company's 20% discount (40,000 yuan), totaling 100,000 yuan, the government receives 100,000 yuan. Combined, Type A and Type B lottery tickets generate a total of 250,000 yuan for the government each month. (July 4th)

Continued Report on the Wuhu French Concession Lawsuit 98

Higher Court Sends Personnel to Investigate

Wuhu Correspondence: The Wuhu Lawyers Association has accused Pei Xiyu and Da Shiying, judges of the local court, and Li Weixin and She Honghao, two lawyers, of malfeasance, embezzlement, and bribery. The association resolutely reported them, ordering the expulsion of the two lawyers She and Li from the association, and submitting accusations to the Control Yuan, the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and the Anhui Higher Court. Thus, a major disturbance has arisen between the legal profession and the judiciary. Zeng Youhao, the president of the Anhui Higher Court, traveled from the province to Beijing and made a special stop in Wuhu to investigate the matter, and also dispatched Sheng Shibi, a prosecutor from the Higher Court's Procuratorate, to Wuhu to conduct a preliminary investigation into the truth of the case. After She and Li were expelled from the Lawyers Association, She alone accused Zhang Benyi and Huang Jing, the drafters of the accusation submitted to various parties by the Lawyers Association, of smoking opium. She also accused Ge Fenglai, the president of the Lawyers Association, and members Hu Baisha and Huang Jing of abuse of power and obstruction of rights. Li Weixin, for his part, also accused President Ge Fenglai of obstructing the exercise of his rights. It is truly a complex and tumultuous lawsuit. The court considered the accusation of obstructing rights to be an act of judicial administration and dismissed the case. The court immediately accepted the accusation of opium smoking. After Huang Jing arrived at the court, he underwent 74 hours of examination, and no signs of opium addiction were found. He continued to draft documents, hold discussions, and perform his duties as usual. As a result, various witnesses, the court, the bailiffs, and Lawyer She Honghao all agreed that there was no need for further examination. Yesterday, Cui Xiangqiu, the former president of the Lawyers Association, Ge Fenglai, the current president, and Chen Ya arrived at the court together to welcome Huang out. At this time, Zhang Benyi, another lawyer accused of smoking opium, suddenly returned from Shanghai and went to the court to surrender. He stated that the prosecutor handling the case, Pei Xiyu, was one of the defendants accused by the Lawyers Association and should be recused. The court accepted this and reassigned Prosecutor Li Yucang to conduct the interrogation today. Zhang stated that he does not smoke opium, and that She, resentful of the fact that he was one of the drafters of the accusations by the Lawyers Association, was intentionally retaliating. He also argued that the court's issuance of an arrest warrant without first issuing a summons was unlawful and requested that a doctor be appointed to examine him in order to protect his reputation. It is reported that the Higher Court believes that this case has a significant impact on the judiciary and is determined to investigate it thoroughly. Due to the complexity of the case, it is planned to hold the trial in Wuhu for the sake of convenience. (6th)

Zhang, an Adopted Daughter-in-Law, Escapes Back After Being Abducted 105

Zhang, an adopted daughter-in-law with the nickname Qiaogu, from the twenty-third district of the county, was abducted and sold three years ago by Huang Apu, a local rogue, to a brothel in Hankou. Later, fortunately, Zhu Hanzhong, a carpenter from the same village, rescued her from the fire pit and remarried her as a concubine to You Pusheng, a cigarette broker. Unexpectedly, You recently failed in business and came to Shanghai to make a living. Forced by food and clothing, he mortgaged his wife to Hu Huogen, a Tianjin native, for 200 yuan. Hu then hired someone to sell her to another port, but Zhang, having experienced great hardship, regretted her past mistakes. Therefore, she took a boat back yesterday and went directly to her husband's house, kneeling down and begging for forgiveness. Finally, the relatives of both parties reconciled, and they were reunited. One party, after the incident, reported Zhang's kidnapping by Huang Apu to the county court today, requesting that he be punished according to the law.

Wuxi

The Department of Construction recently received instructions from the Ministry of Industry, stating that the central government clearly ordered the abolition of transit taxes in consideration of the people's livelihood, and commodity prices in various places should be low in order to live up to the government's intention to abolish transit taxes. Master Dixian Comes to Wuxi to Give Lectures 107

The Wuxi County Buddhist Association, Puren Charity Association, and Red Swastika Society recently jointly organized a Puli Taoist Temple for the soldiers who died in the Northern Expedition. They specially invited the eminent contemporary master Dixian to come and give lectures. After the period, he will return to Hangzhou to give lectures. It is said that the Master will no longer participate in any kind of religious events after this.

Gaoqiao Tailor Shop Robbed 108

Xu Ahuan's tailor shop at No. 19 Gaoqiao, Tonghui Road, was suddenly visited by two robbers with weapons after 10 p.m. the other night. Ahuan happened to be out collecting debts. The robbers drove his wife and children into a corner of the room, swept away the clothing materials in the room, and lost about one hundred yuan.

Changzhou

Losses from Continuous Heavy Rain 109

Wuyi has been experiencing continuous heavy rain recently, and the low-lying fields have become a swamp. The river water has risen sharply, causing great panic among residents along the banks. Before the rain, the price of rice was about nine yuan per load. It rose to nine yuan, eight or nine cents the previous two days. Starting from the 10th, it has been sold for ten yuan and six cents. If the weather does not clear up and goods do not arrive from the river, prices are expected to rise further. Near Qishuyan in the eastern countryside, Wang Xiaolong's boat collided with Chen's black bean boat the other night due to the rapid water flow. Chen and his wife and children fell into the river. Xiao Long stopped his boat to rescue them. Chen and his wife and two sons were rescued, but his three-year-old daughter was dead when she was pulled out of the water. The beans and rice in the boat sank or floated away. Furthermore, a Changzhou-Wuxi express boat carrying fifteen pieces of tin foil also capsized near Yangqiao浜. Although it was recovered, the tin foil was damaged by water and was useless, resulting in a loss of about one thousand six hundred yuan.

Zhenjiang

Further Appointment of Ganyu and Guanyun County Magistrates 110

Yesterday, the Jiangsu Provincial Government ordered the dismissal of Lu Kai, the magistrate of Ganyu County, and transferred Yan Xifang, the magistrate of Guanyun County, to succeed him. The vacancy in Guanyun was filled by Li Jin, the second-place candidate in the county magistrate examination.

Nantong

The Tide of Opening the Dikes in the Eastern Countryside Subsides 111

In the eighth district of Nantong's eastern countryside, a large flood occurred. Villagers upstream and downstream, due to conflicting interests regarding opening the dikes, engaged in armed fighting. The defense corps of each district also joined the vortex, firing guns and killing several people. As the turmoil escalated, the county government strictly prohibited the defense corps from mobilizing without authorization. Technicians from the Construction Bureau were dispatched to investigate and negotiate with the district chiefs to properly handle the aftermath and opened the Huanben and Yaowang gates along the coast and dug up the dams to relieve the flood victims upstream.

Deep-Water Port's Shore Construction Controversy Resolved 112

The villagers in Langshan Deepwater Port opposed the Construction Bureau's requisitioning of the river to build a receding bank, resulting in conflicts with the police. Injuries occurred on both sides. The county government arrested fifteen ringleaders, including Ni Panzi. The villagers sued the police in court, leading to unresolved disputes. Through mediation by various parties, the receding bank project continues, the lawsuit is withdrawn, and Ni Panzi and others were released from the county government on the night of the 8th.

Chamber of Commerce Acknowledges Business Tax Payment 113

The Nantong County Chamber of Commerce acknowledged paying 32,000 yuan in business tax for the entire year, which was handled by various trade associations. 3,600 yuan has already been paid to the province.

Huzhou

Cloth Industry Dispute Resolved 114

The Dingxin Cloth Shop in the north street of this city was opening and offering discounted items. The deadline was overdue, causing disputes among the same industry. Subsequently, after the Chamber of Commerce mediated, the Dingxin shop was still reluctant to accept. The court inspected the situation. It is now learned that at 9 p.m. yesterday, the Wuxing County Chamber of Commerce held a temporary meeting. County Magistrate Li Guangyu and more than 40 people including Tan Jianchen, Shao Shoumin, and Hang Kuiqing attended. The cloth industry discussed the matter for a long time, and decided to fine Yichengxing Yang 200 yuan to help the orphanage. The initial agreement of 300 yuan for the relief of the Wubao was changed to 200 yuan, which was used to help the nursery. It was also agreed that the discounted items would not exceed three. Both parties were satisfied and dispersed. The dispute was thus resolved.

Defaulted Funds and Fleeing Accumulate Bankruptcies 115

After Zhu Weide, director of the Wuxing County Chao Character Mortgage Gold, defaulted on a large sum of money and fled, the county government issued an arrest warrant and ordered the original guarantor, Zhu Binshi, to compensate the full amount. All of Zhu Binshi's properties were seized. It is now learned that yesterday (8th) at 3 p.m., personnel Tang E, Zhang Zhongheng, and others, along with Hang Kuiqing, a representative of the County Chamber of Commerce, went to Yangjia Lane outside the North Gate to unseal Zhu Binshi's Zhuxiechang winery. The entire winery's equipment, about 80 items, was listed and priced and will be auctioned soon.

Bandit Luo Haishan Executed by Firing Squad 116

Luo Youshan, the bandit escorted to the Wuxing Local Court by the Water Police Detachment, was the ringleader in the kidnapping of the monk He Jin. During the trial, Xu Deming of the Water Police Detachment and the kidnapped monk He Jin testified in court that he was indeed the perpetrator and was sentenced to death. The Higher Court approved the execution by firing squad. At 11 a.m. today, Chief Prosecutor Pan supervised the extraction of the criminal, verified his identity, and escorted him to the South Schoolyard in this city for execution by firing squad.

Ningbo

Reconnaissance of the Yongbu Airfield Completed 117

Huang Bingheng, Director of the Central Aviation Administration, specially dispatched Adjutant Guo Muhan to Yongbo the other day to inspect the airfield. It is now learned that after Guo arrived in Yongbo, he found an open space facing west in Wangjiawan, measuring more than 400 mu. Furthermore, because it is close to Yao River and Beidou Lake, seaplanes can also land easily. Therefore, it was considered suitable, and it was decided to build the airfield there. He returned around 10 o'clock and returned to Beijing this afternoon to report back to facilitate early construction.

Shaoxing

Tangpu Sailing Ship Robbed 118

The sailing ship operating between Tangpu and Baiguan was leaving Tangpu on the night before last. There were more than ten passengers on board, mostly small business owners. When the ship was about to leave, two people in short clothes got off the boat, but no one paid much attention at the time. Unexpectedly, at around 10 o'clock, when the ship sailed to Xiaogang, two burly men suddenly appeared on the shore and ordered the captain to stop the ship. At the same time, two passengers on the ship pulled out their pistols and fired into the sky, ordering the ship to dock. The captain had no choice but to comply. The four bandits then joined forces to search the passengers, robbing them of a total of hundreds of gold. They then went ashore and escaped. The captain sailed the boat back to Tangpu and reported it to the authorities for arrest.

Xiaoshan

Another Kidnapping Case in Dayi Village 119

Wang Guisheng, son of Wang Jiarong, the owner of Wang Yixing Rice Shop in Dayi Village in Xiaoshan's eastern countryside, was suddenly kidnapped from his bed by more than ten bandits on the night of the 5th. Before leaving, they fired two shots in the air as a warning. Yesterday, a letter was sent to his family demanding 50,000 yuan in foreign currency for his release.

A Large Number of Refugees Entering the Territory Causing Disturbance 120

On the afternoon of the 5th, more than a hundred refugees suddenly arrived in Nanshatou Peng Town, speaking with a Hunan accent. The refugee representatives asked the shops in the town for food and lodging. After the shops paid six yuan for food, they were allowed to live in the Niangniang Temple. Furthermore, on the 7th, 70 refugees arrived in Jiudun, extorting money and goods from door to door, creating a tense situation. The residents were very afraid. Local gentry and wealthy people paid five yuan and two dou of white rice, and they went to Anchang.

Two Directors Take Office Successively 121

The newly appointed Director Zheng of the Xiaoshan County Public Security Bureau arrived in Xiaoshan on the 5th and officially took office today (9th). Furthermore, Director He Zhengrong of the Construction Bureau was ordered to be transferred to the province. The newly appointed Director Huang Chao also arrived in Xiaoshan on the 7th and officially took office on the 8th.

Hurricane Sinks Boats and Drowns Boatmen 122

At about 8 p.m. on the 8th, a hurricane suddenly struck. The boats in the Qiantang River were unable to dock in time and were all sunk. Two fishing boats in Dongjiangzui were in the middle of the river when their masts were broken by the wind and they sank immediately. Nine boatmen drowned, two of whom died. Furthermore, two altar boats loaded with goods came from Xixiaojiang Yulinguan in the inner river and were blown against the stone embankment by the wind at Xieen Bridge. The boats were broken and water flowed into the cabin, sinking them instantly. Four boatmen shouted for help. Fortunately, nearby fishing boats tried their best to rescue them, rescuing two people. It is thought that the other two also drowned.

Liaoyang

Tragedy of Four Deaths from Poisoning 123

In Zhang Yisan's comb shop in Nan Shuidong, Liaoyang City, there were two sons and two daughters. The eldest son, in his twenties, is currently a prosecutor in the Yingkou Court and lives in Yingkou with his family. The second son, 12, the eldest daughter, 19, and the second daughter, 15, all lived at home with their parents. Years ago, the eldest daughter had an affair with her apprentice Zhang Shuxi (currently 32 years old, from Hejian County, Hebei Province) (which has been confirmed by the court) and made a lifelong commitment. However, Zhang's wife did not agree and dismissed him, hiring another apprentice. Zhang Shuxi harbored resentment and sought revenge, but continued to feign friendship and often visited his home. On July 3rd, he bought half a catty of red alum in the city and secretly mixed it into Zhang's family's biscuits and [unclear]. After dinner, the whole family discovered that they had been poisoned. The eldest daughter, second son, and apprentice died one after another at night. His wife and second daughter were less severely affected and were sent to the public hospital for treatment on the morning of the 4th. His wife also died in the afternoon. The life of the second daughter may be saved. After the case occurred, it was reported to the Public Security Bureau, and Zhang Shuxi has been detained and transferred to the local court for handling. Fortunately, Zhang Yisan and his eldest son were not at home when the case occurred, otherwise [unclear] would have been killed.

Letter

Letter from the Jiangsu Provincial Capital Construction Engineering Office 124

Dear Sir, We are writing to address the case of He Bingsen, the owner of Heyuanji Woodwork, who was found to have used old city bricks in the wall of the Hongxing Pool construction on Zhongshan Road. This office thoroughly investigated and found evidence that He Bingsen, the owner of Heyuanji Woodwork, claimed that the bricks were obtained at a price after dismantling the wall of the Security Office Prison, and that when moving the broken bricks when paving the floor of the Finance Department, these bricks were sorted out and there were only a few. Because the He Bingsen, the owner of Heyuanji Woodwork, was suspected of using public property, he was immediately punished by constructing a public project worth one hundred yuan, and He Bingsen submitted a written guarantee on file. Your newspaper published an article on the 6th of this month that this office would punish He Bingsen, the owner of Heyuanji Woodwork, for stealing city bricks and would be fined 4,000 yuan for confiscation. This is not in accordance with the facts. This letter is specially sent to request a correction. Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction, Provincial Capital Construction Engineering Office, July 8th.

Education News

Important News

Jiangsu Province's 20th Annual Education Budget (6) Shi Zhang 125

(6) Review of the Implementation of Last Year's Budget

The actual and possible budgets for this year have been discussed in detail by the reporter yesterday. Of course, a mere ideal estimation of last year's income and expenditure does not fully conform to the actual situation. Now, let’s make a precise calculation based on the monthly income and expenditure reports published by the Education Fund Management Office. In this way, the reality of last year's budget can be obtained here. However, up to the most recent time, the income and expenditure reports of the management office have only been printed and published until March of this year, and the reports for the three months of April, May, and June have not yet come out, so there is no way to guess their numbers. But there is also a remedy, which is to add up the actual income and expenditure figures for the nine months from June of last year to March of this year, and calculate the average number. This average number is equivalent to the monthly value of the other three months (April, May, June). Although it is not completely accurate, it may be roughly similar. The actual income, expenditure, and balance of the nine months are listed below:

Total for Nine Months Three, One Five Eight, Seven Four Nine, One Six Three, One Zero Nine, Five Six One, Four Nine Four Nine, One Eight Seven, Six Seven The remaining balance of the above item, plus the balance for June, is exactly One Three Nine, Seven One Six, Zero Six, which is the same as the balance for March.

Let us look at the table on the right. The total income for the nine months is more than 3,158,749 yuan, with an average of more than 50,972 yuan per month. Assuming that the total income for the three months of April, May, and June is 1,052,916 yuan, then the total income for the whole year will be 4,211,665 yuan. (The reporter assumed yesterday that the annual income would be less than 4,300,000 yuan, and the difference seems to be small.) As for the expenditure, of course, the situation is the same. As long as we understand the actual income and expenditure situation in the past, we can imagine the general trend in the future. The reporter sincerely prays for the success of the Jiangsu Province's 20th Annual Education Budget, and will discuss its progress in detail with readers on this day next year. (End)

Shanxi College of Politics and Law Cannot be Changed to a Law School 128

Order to Close Down Gradually Year by Year

The Ministry of Education, according to the request from the Shanxi Provincial Government to change the Shanxi Public College of Politics and Law into a Law School, was unable to approve it. It especially replied to the Provincial Government, stating: According to your government's Jia Zi No. 30 letter, the Education Department presented the reasons for the Shanxi Public College of Politics and Law to be changed into the Shanxi Provincial Law School and its reorganization. The Ministry replied that, considering that setting up schools in the same area should avoid duplication and save expenses, Shanxi University in your province already has a Law School. The Shanxi Public College of Politics and Law should temporarily follow the Ministry's school suspension method and order to close down gradually year by year. The request to change it into a Provincial Law School cannot be approved.

Municipal Education Bureau Announces Rules for Supervising Summer Schools 133

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau had previously stated that there were a large number of summer schools established by schools at all levels in the city, and it was urgent to formulate rules to follow. Therefore, it drafted the rules for supervising summer schools and submitted them to the Ministry of Education for review. The Ministry has now approved the filing and ordered the schools to comply. The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's rules for supervising summer schools are copied below: (1) These rules shall apply to all summer schools established in the city, and the Bureau shall supervise them. (2) The students admitted to the summer school shall comply with the Ministry's order that the students of secondary schools and above, teachers, or other civil servants shall be limited. (3) The academic performance of students in the summer school shall not be used as formal credits or term of study, according to the Ministry's order. (4) The tuition fee for summer schools shall be limited to one yuan for each subject per week of instruction for universities, and five cents for middle schools. If the instruction is more than one hour, it shall be increased accordingly. (5) Elementary schools may set up summer remedial classes, and the fee for each student shall be limited to one yuan per term. (6) To establish a summer school, the founder shall fill out a form with the following items and submit it to the Bureau for approval: 1. Name; 2. School address; 3. Purpose (for teachers or civil servants to improve their skills or for students to make up for their studies); 4. Name, resume, and address of the founder; 5. List of principals and faculty members; 6. List of academic programs; When submitting the application, a copy of the articles of association must also be attached. (7) The Bureau will send personnel to inspect the summer school at any time. If there is any violation of these rules or other inappropriate matters, it may be subject to restrictions. (8) The summer school shall report the names of the students and the grades of each subject to the Bureau for record when the study ends. (9) These rules shall be announced and implemented after being submitted to the Ministry of Education for record.

Private Schools Must Complete the Registration Procedures as Soon as Possible 136

Beyond the Deadline… Municipal Education Bureau Strictly Bans According to the Ministry's Order

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has repeatedly issued announcements and dispatched personnel to urge private schools in Shanghai that have not been registered. In February of this year, the Municipal Education Bureau received an order from the Ministry of Education to complete the registration procedures for private schools that have not yet been registered before the first day of the first semester of the 20th year. If they still fail to do so after the deadline, they will be strictly banned. The Municipal Education Bureau has re-examined the registration forms and ordered each unregistered private school to comply and printed a notice to distribute to all unregistered private schools at all levels to comply. It is heard that a large number of schools have recently applied for registration in accordance with the regulations. The first semester of the 20th year is approaching. If there are any schools that have not yet applied, they should complete the registration procedures within the deadline. If they continue to wait and see beyond this final deadline, the Municipal Education Bureau will have no choice but to follow the Ministry's order and strictly ban them in order to emphasize the law.

"Discussion Collection on Life's Problems" Essay Contest 137

Mr. Xu Wancheng is about to compile a "Discussion Collection on Life's Problems." Now, an essay contest is being held with five topics: (1) My Difficulties and Struggles in Pursuing Higher Education; (2) A Discussion of My Work Experience; (3) My Views on Divorce; (4) The Reasons Why I Support the Big Family System or the Small Family System; (5) My Proposal for a Wedding Ceremony. All young people are encouraged to write enthusiastically. The deadline is the end of July.

It is also stipulated that listeners who are absent for more than a quarter of the time will not be allowed to take the final exam. Davis Cup European Zone Final 142

British Maple Pole Advantage

丨Two Singles All Win Against Czech Republic丨

Prague, 9th Telegram 143

Britain is almost certain to win the Davis Cup European-American Zone final, and will compete with the United States for the Challege Round. Both singles were won decisively against the Czech Republic.

Results of the First and Second Singles Matches 144

Austin (England) 3-6, 6-2, 6-8, 6-3, 6-2 Meng Ruier (Czech)

Bailey (England) 6-1, 8-6, 6-3 Haxied (Czech)

British Players Return to Original State 145

In today's two singles matches, Austin's victory was not easy. Meng Ruier put on strong pressure, but Austin's perseverance and determination ultimately led to victory. Although Meng took a 2-1 lead, Austin became more and more courageous as the match progressed, and the final highlights were even more numerous. His victory was entirely due to his extremely resolute determination. In the second singles match, Bailey's victory over Haxied was without much contention. Bailey's straight-set victory showed that the British players had fully returned to their original state. Although they were in a foreign land, their spirit was even better than in the Wimbledon tournament, and the championship situation was looming.

Interest Focused on the Anglo-American Decisive Battle 146

With Britain's elimination of the Czech Republic already a settled fact, all interest is now focused on next week's Anglo-American zonal final to win the right to challenge France. The United States has won the Challege Round for four consecutive years, while Britain has not won it since 1919. The Davis Cup was last won in 1912. In total, the United States has won the cup 10 times, Britain 5 times, Australia 6 times, and France 4 times.

Judging from the performance of the American team members in the Wimbledon tournament, the United States still holds the advantage in the Anglo-American zonal final. Van Lenlood's doubles are probably insurmountable for Britain, and Hills Wood's singles are also likely to win.

Scheduled Triangular Swimming Competition 148

Participants Include China, America, and Japan

丨Evening of July 25th in Xiqing丨

The Xiqing YMCA will launch a swimming competition, as reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday, the association invited Yu Binqi of the Chinese Swimming Research Association and Koga of the Japanese Athletic Association to discuss the matter. Under the chairmanship of Topping, the Xiqing affairs officer, the following items were decided:

Name 149

The name is set as Triangular Swimming Competition, without the word "international" because the scope is too large.

Date 150

8:00 p.m. on July 25th.

Location 151

Swimming pool of the Xiqing YMCA on Jing'an Temple Road.

Programs 152

Nine events including 50-yard freestyle, 100-yard freestyle, 200-yard freestyle, 880-yard freestyle, 100-yard backstroke, 100-yard breaststroke, 200-yard medley, 150-yard three-style medley, and fancy diving.

Scoring 153

Take the top four places, using a scoring system of 5, 3, 2, and 1, i.e., the first place gets 5 points, and the fourth place gets 1 point.

Prizes 154

One gold medal for the first place, one silver medal for the second place, one bronze medal for the third place, and none for the fourth place for now.

The Still Strong Xue Rubo, Long-Distance Runner 155

Aged 53丨Overwhelms Famous Leg Lang Bodo丨

A letter from Toron Tu, England, today (June 13th): Two famous long-distance runners held a competition locally. One is Alpha Lai Xue Rubo, now 53 years old. At that time, more than a thousand spectators recalled Mr. Xue's golden age twenty years ago, giving rise to the idea of a hero who is still strong in his old age. His opponent, Tom Lang Bodo, is a famous marathon runner from North America. The one-mile finish line was crossed by Mr. Xue twenty-five yards ahead, winning countless praises. Many of the world and British amateur records between two and ten miles are still held by Mr. Xue.

Resolution of the Bonus and Housing Problems of Chinese Electric Workers 178

Bonus...5% of 30% of Net Profit

Housing...Annual Subsidy of 10,000 Yuan

The Chinese electrical workers of the city have been passively striking due to the company's lack of sincerity in resolving the housing and bonus issues, with trains running without ticket sales. The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs scheduled a mediation for yesterday, but the labor and management sides had already reached an agreement and signed a resolution on their own the night before. The situation is recorded below.

Negotiation Situation 179

At 9:00 a.m. on the 9th, the First District Water and Electricity Industry Union sent responsible representatives Zhou Guangrong, Tang Junsheng, Zhu Hanhe, Fang Ronggeng, Jia Renjie, and others to negotiate with Lu Bohong, manager of the Huashang Electric Company, and representatives Yao Xinzhi and Zhu Shaoyi, among others, on the workers' bonuses and housing issues. Because the union obeyed the workers' will, it requested the company to allocate 200,000 yuan to purchase land to build workers' housing, to be completed by the end of 20 years. Before the construction is completed, the company will issue a housing allowance of 10 yuan per month to each person. The board of directors will be responsible for proposing the bonus from the 20th year onwards, and the shareholders' meeting will approve that the workers' share of the annual net profit should not be less than 21.96%, of which 60% will be used exclusively for the labor cause fund, and the remaining 40% will be distributed to the workers according to the size of their wages. The company insisted on not acknowledging this. Until 7:00 p.m., the labor side repeatedly made concessions in order to maintain their inherent feelings, and the issue was finally resolved.

Resolution 180

The original text of the worker bonus and housing issues resolved by mutual agreement and signing between the labor and management sides of the Huashang Electric Company is as follows: (1) The company shall not provide less than 5% of 30% of the net profit each year as a bonus for the workers, to be handed over to the union for distribution. (2) The company shall provide 10,000 yuan in national currency each year as a special subsidy, to be handed over to the union each month for equal distribution to all workers. (All supplementary negotiation clauses will be added when the contract is signed, and will be implemented from June 1st of this year.) Regarding the company's request to amend Article 6 of the signed labor-management treaty on pensions, the union agreed to add an explanation of the length of service of new employees in the supplementary clauses, and both parties will submit the documents to the Bureau of Social Affairs for verification.

Shuang Qing Discusses the Incident of the Eurasian Aircraft Landing in Outer Mongolia 181

Constantly Believing… It Occurred Within Our Own Territory

The Proper Solution… Request the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission for Rescue

Following the forced landing of a Eurasian Aviation Corporation plane in Outer Mongolia, Mr. Shuang Qing, the general manager of the company, made the following statement yesterday: (1) The reason and location of the plane's landing, according to telegrams, the landing point is 248 kilometers south of Manzhouli, southeast of Lake Baikal, which is within our national border. There do not appear to be any national troops stationed there. The reason for the forced landing has not yet been reported in detail, but it is speculated that it was due to the adverse weather conditions, forcing a landing, resulting in detention by Mongolian soldiers. The transportation is inconvenient, and the pilot has been unable to report the news to the company. (2) The current rescue methods, the company immediately reported to the Ministry of Communications upon receiving the telegram. Now, it has submitted a request to the Ministry of Communications, requesting the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission to find ways to rescue them, so that they can be released as soon as possible. Perhaps the local authorities in Outer Mongolia are not clear about the true situation of the postal aviation run by our company. This action may have arisen from a misunderstanding. It is expected that once the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission sends a telegram to explain, there will be no problems. As for the news that the German staff of our company in Peiping have asked the German consulates in China to intercede with the Soviet Union for rescue, this may be a rumor or a misunderstanding. Perhaps the German consulate, considering that the detained pilots and workers are all German nationals, is seeking to rescue these two Germans, and, out of friendly relations, is asking the Soviet consulate nearby to help. It is possible, but our company constantly believes that this matter occurred in the Outer Mongolian region of Chinese territory, and has absolutely no connection to diplomatic relations. The only proper solution is to ask the Ministry of Communications to request the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission to explain and rescue them. As for the No. 1 and No. 3 planes sent to search, they flew back to Peiping from Manzhouli on the 9th via the original route, and no obstacles occurred. It can be seen that the No. 2 plane's accident was also accidental, or there is no other background. We cannot regard a temporary event as a major issue, and engage in overly sensitive speculation, which would only create further complications. As for the Berlin special dispatch, stating that the German Foreign Office has begun negotiations with the Soviet Foreign Office, it is probably also about the rescue of German pilots and seeking Soviet friendship, and it is definitely not about specific negotiations regarding this matter, etc.
